( /* Subselect from SDE_ORA_GLAccountDimension.W_GL_ACCOUNT_DS
*/

	   FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL.ID_FLEX_NUM	AS ID_FLEX_NUM,

from	((APPS.FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL  LEFT OUTER JOIN  APPS.FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_S  
    ON  FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL.APPLICATION_ID=FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_S.APPLICATION_ID
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL.ID_FLEX_NUM=FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_S.ID_FLEX_NUM
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL.ID_FLEX_CODE=FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_S.ID_FLEX_CODE
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL.APPLICATION_COLUMN_NAME = FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_S.APPLICATION_COLUMN_NAME
     )  LEFT OUTER JOIN  APPS.FND_FLEX_VALUE_SETS PARENT_CC_VALUESET_SQ_BCI_GL_A  
    ON  FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL.FLEX_VALUE_SET_ID=PARENT_CC_VALUESET_SQ_BCI_GL_A.FLEX_VALUE_SET_ID
     )  LEFT OUTER JOIN  APPS.FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS PARENT_CC_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL_AC  
    ON  FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL.APPLICATION_ID=PARENT_CC_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL_AC.APPLICATION_ID
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL.ID_FLEX_NUM=PARENT_CC_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL_AC.ID_FLEX_NUM
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL.ID_FLEX_CODE=PARENT_CC_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL_AC.ID_FLEX_CODE
AND 
PARENT_CC_VALUESET_SQ_BCI_GL_A.PARENT_FLEX_VALUE_SET_ID=PARENT_CC_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL_AC.FLEX_VALUE_SET_ID
where	(1=1)
 and (FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_S.SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_TYPE='FA_COST_CTR' AND 
FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_S.ATTRIBUTE_VALUE='Y') and (FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL.APPLICATION_ID=101 AND FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI_GL.ID_FLEX_CODE='GL#')
)  COST_CENTER_SQ_BCI_GL_ACCOUNTS  
    ON  GL_CODE_COMBINATIONS_SQ_BCI_GL.CHART_OF_ACCOUNTS_ID=COST_CENTER_SQ_BCI_GL_ACCOUNTS.ID_FLEX_NUM
     )  LEFT OUTER JOIN  
( /* Subselect from SDE_ORA_GLAccountDimension.W_GL_ACCOUNT_DS
*/

select 
	  

	   FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__1.ID_FLEX_NUM	AS ID_FLEX_NUM,

from	APPS.FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__1  LEFT OUTER JOIN  APPS.FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_1  
    ON  FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__1.APPLICATION_ID=FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_1.APPLICATION_ID
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__1.ID_FLEX_NUM=FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_1.ID_FLEX_NUM
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__1.ID_FLEX_CODE=FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_1.ID_FLEX_CODE
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__1.APPLICATION_COLUMN_NAME = FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_1.APPLICATION_COLUMN_NAME
where	(1=1)
 and (FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_1.SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_TYPE='GL_BALANCING' AND 
FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_1.ATTRIBUTE_VALUE='Y') and (FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__1.APPLICATION_ID=101 AND FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__1.ID_FLEX_CODE='GL#')
)  BALANCING_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL_AC  
    ON  GL_CODE_COMBINATIONS_SQ_BCI_GL.CHART_OF_ACCOUNTS_ID=BALANCING_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL_AC.ID_FLEX_NUM
     )  LEFT OUTER JOIN  
( /* Subselect from SDE_ORA_GLAccountDimension.W_GL_ACCOUNT_DS
*/

select 
	  

	   FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2.ID_FLEX_NUM	AS ID_FLEX_NUM,
	FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2.FLEX_VALUE_SET_ID	AS NA_VALUE_SET_ID,
	FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2.APPLICATION_COLUMN_NAME	AS NA_SEGMENT,
	PARENT_CC_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL__1.APPLICATION_COLUMN_NAME	AS NA_PARENT_SEGMENT,
	FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_2.LAST_UPDATE_DATE	AS LAST_UPDATE_DATE
from	((APPS.FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2  LEFT OUTER JOIN  APPS.FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_2  
    ON  FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2.APPLICATION_ID=FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_2.APPLICATION_ID
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2.ID_FLEX_NUM=FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_2.ID_FLEX_NUM
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2.ID_FLEX_CODE=FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_2.ID_FLEX_CODE
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2.APPLICATION_COLUMN_NAME = FND_SEGMENT_ATTRIBUTE_VALUES_2.APPLICATION_COLUMN_NAME
     )  LEFT OUTER JOIN  APPS.FND_FLEX_VALUE_SETS PARENT_CC_VALUESET_SQ_BCI_GL_1  
    ON  FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2.FLEX_VALUE_SET_ID=PARENT_CC_VALUESET_SQ_BCI_GL_1.FLEX_VALUE_SET_ID
     )  LEFT OUTER JOIN  APPS.FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS PARENT_CC_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL__1  
    ON  FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2.APPLICATION_ID=PARENT_CC_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL__1.APPLICATION_ID
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2.ID_FLEX_NUM=PARENT_CC_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL__1.ID_FLEX_NUM
AND 
FND_ID_FLEX_SEGMENTS_SQ_BCI__2.ID_FLEX_CODE=PARENT_CC_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL__1.ID_FLEX_CODE
AND 
PARENT_CC_VALUESET_SQ_BCI_GL_1.PARENT_FLEX_VALUE_SET_ID=PARENT_CC_SEGMENT_SQ_BCI_GL__1.FLEX_VALUE_SET_ID

                      THEN  'AUTOCORRECT_STRING'
                      WHEN IND_UPDATE IN ('I','S', 'U') AND (DIAGNOSTIC_ROWID IS NULL AND ORA_ERR_TAG$ ='__INSERT_I$_ERROR__') and AUTOCORRECT_IND = 'Y'
                      THEN   'INSERT_UNSPECIFIED'
                      WHEN UPPER(ORA_ERR_TAG$) LIKE ('%DUPLICATE%') and ERROR_TYPE_IND NOT IN ('TARG_FULL_DUPE1', 'I$DUPE1')  and AUTOCORRECT_IND = 'N'
                      THEN   'REJECT_DUPLICATE'
                      ELSE 
                      'REJECT_DATA_ISSUE'
                      END, 
AUTOCORRECT_DESC = CASE 
                      WHEN ORA_ERR_TAG$ IN ('Duplicate Check in Target in Full Load', '__DUPLICATE_CHECK_I$__') and ERROR_TYPE_IND IN ('TARG_FULL_DUPE1', 'I$DUPE1')  and AUTOCORRECT_IND = 'Y' 
                      THEN 'This row is one of the duplicates found for this target table. One of the duplicate rows will be inserted, and all others will be rejected. This row will be inserted.'
                      WHEN ORA_ERR_TAG$ IN ('__INSERT_I$_ERROR__', '__INSERT_REPLICA_ERRORS__') and  ORA_ERR_NUMBER$ = '12899'  and AUTOCORRECT_IND = 'Y'
                      THEN    'This row has one or more string/varchar columns with more characters than allowed. All such strings will be trimmed to fit the target table.'    
                      WHEN IND_UPDATE IN ('I','S', 'U') AND (DIAGNOSTIC_ROWID IS NULL AND ORA_ERR_TAG$ ='__INSERT_I$_ERROR__')  and AUTOCORRECT_IND = 'Y'
                      THEN   'This row has unidentified data issues that could not be handled/corrected. This row will still be inserted with dummy/unspecified values for all columns except the primary key columns.'
                      WHEN UPPER(ORA_ERR_TAG$) LIKE ('%DUPLICATE%') and ERROR_TYPE_IND NOT IN ('TARG_FULL_DUPE1', 'I$DUPE1')  and AUTOCORRECT_IND = 'N'

                      ELSE

                      END;

END IF;

	END;

	    EXIT;
	END IF;
    END LOOP;
  END;

    v_EVENT_RESULT := v_EVENT_RESULT || ' ResourceBusy Wait between: ' || 600*(v_loopctr-1) ||'-'|| 600*v_loopctr || ' seconds';
  END IF;
  COMMIT;

  NULL;
END;
